    function setAttributeOnload(object, attribute, val) {
      if(window.addEventListener) {
        window.addEventListener('load',
          function(){ object[attribute] = val; }, false);
      } else {
        window.attachEvent('onload', function(){ object[attribute] = val; });
      }
    }

$(document).ready(function(){
var first = 0;
var speed = 200;
var pause = 2400;
function removeFirst(){
first = $('ul#slide li:first').html();
$('ul#slide li:first')
.animate({opacity: 0.5}, speed)
.fadeOut('slow', function() {$(this).remove();});
addLast(first);
}
function addLast(first){
last = '<li style="display:none">'+first+'</li>';
$('ul#slide').append(last)
$('ul#slide li:last')
.animate({opacity: 1}, speed)
.fadeIn('slow')
}
interval = setInterval(removeFirst, pause);
});
</script>

<h2 class='date-header'><span>sexta-feira, 12 de abril de 2013</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry'>
<a name='7782262860288885886'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='http://www.celebrinando.com/2013/04/yahoo-mente-e-diz-que-panicat-sofreu.html'>Yahoo mente e diz que Nicole Bahls sofreu "Abuso Sexual" durante entrevista</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-7782262860288885886'>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-WFXrM8-97xc/UWfV3DhkbyI/AAAAAAAADiQ/fHeW4Nc6pAA/s1600/nicole1.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="417" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-WFXrM8-97xc/UWfV3DhkbyI/AAAAAAAADiQ/fHeW4Nc6pAA/s640/nicole1.PNG" width="640" /></a></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Quem trabalha com jornalismo de celebridade sabe que uma boa chamada para sua nota garante bons cliques, mas tudo tem limite, e muitas das vezes essa tara por acessos faz grandes sites extrapolarem a linha do bom senso.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Foi o caso do portal <b>Yahoo Brasil</b> que noticiou que a ex-panicat, agora&nbsp;repÃ³rter<b>&nbsp;</b><span style="line-height: 17.99715805053711px;"><b>Nicole Bahls</b>, sofreu "Abuso Sexual" durante entrevista para o Programa Panico. Veja as chamadas laterais nos sites do portal:</span></span><br />
<span style="color: #666666; font-family: arial; font-size: 11.818181991577148px; line-height: 17.99715805053711px;"><br /></span>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YnLQnSYV48k/UWfW_LynJTI/AAAAAAAADic/6YhDVqfS3mY/s1600/yahoo1.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="410" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-YnLQnSYV48k/UWfW_LynJTI/AAAAAAAADic/6YhDVqfS3mY/s640/yahoo1.PNG" width="640" /></a></div>
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TrnFHbleIqQ/UWfW_XTpxPI/AAAAAAAADig/euG3CyF10w4/s1600/yahoo3.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="338" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-TrnFHbleIqQ/UWfW_XTpxPI/AAAAAAAADig/euG3CyF10w4/s640/yahoo3.PNG" width="640" /></a></div>
<span style="color: #666666; font-family: arial; font-size: 11.818181991577148px; line-height: 17.99715805053711px;"><br /></span>
<br />
<br />
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Mas quando&nbsp;vocÃª&nbsp;clica na noticia, a chamada muda, ameniza, e se torna muito mais apropriada ao que realmente aconteceu durante a&nbsp;gravaÃ§Ã£o&nbsp;do&nbsp;humorÃ­stico. Dizendo que diretor enfiou a&nbsp;mÃ£o&nbsp;dentro do vestido da&nbsp;repÃ³rter. Confira:</span><br />
<br />
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-OyCOiC4oE8k/UWfXhxIL2II/AAAAAAAADis/_nVSyl-ZnJA/s1600/yahoo2.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="354" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-OyCOiC4oE8k/UWfXhxIL2II/AAAAAAAADis/_nVSyl-ZnJA/s640/yahoo2.PNG" width="640" /></a></div>
<br />
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #333333; line-height: 20px;">Na noite desta quarta-feira (10), a modelo esteve no lanÃ§amento do livro &#8220;Arranhando a SuperfÃ­cie&#8221;, de&nbsp;</span><strong style="border: 0px; color: #333333; line-height: 20px; list-style: none; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">Gerald Thomas</strong><span style="color: #333333; line-height: 20px;">, em uma livraria do Rio de Janeiro, e foi "atacada" pelo diretor teatral.&nbsp;</span>Na verdade tudo&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;passou de uma brincadeira, constrangedora sim, mas dentro da natureza e da proposta&nbsp;humorÃ­stica&nbsp;do programa.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: #333333; line-height: 20px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b>&#8220;Me desacostumei com esse tipo de humor. Cheguei em casa e fiquei abalada, constrangida. Mas depois, pensei um pouco e acho que faz parte do personagem. Ã uma oportunidade que estou tento de voltar e isso faz parte do programa. Tenho que comeÃ§ar a separar o personagem da vida real"</b>&nbsp;</span></span><br />
<span style="color: #333333; line-height: 20px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span></span>
<span style="color: #333333; line-height: 20px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b>&#8220;Acho que ele Ã© gay assumido. Se fosse homem, com outra intenÃ§Ã£o... <span style="color: #333333; font-family: arial; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20px;"><br /></span>

<a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-C6IzAOwSbAU/UWfYWPWWOfI/AAAAAAAADi4/b0HakoLOUdY/s1600/nicole2.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="392" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-C6IzAOwSbAU/UWfYWPWWOfI/AAAAAAAADi4/b0HakoLOUdY/s640/nicole2.PNG" width="640" /></a></div>

<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">EntÃ£o, chamar isso de "Abuso Sexual"? Eu acho que as vitimas REAIS desse tipo de&nbsp;violÃªncia&nbsp;devem no minimo se sentir ofendidas. Lembrando que brincadeiras e uso inadequado das palavras abuso e estupro&nbsp;jÃ¡&nbsp;criaram&nbsp;vÃ¡rios&nbsp;problemas, como aconteceu com o humorista Rafinha Bastos, que fez uma piada sobre o tema, e com o ator Johnny Depp que se referiu a um ensaio sensual que tinha feito, como se a experiencia tivesse sido "um estupro".&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Depois de protestos de ativistas, que reclamaram da&nbsp;banalizaÃ§Ã£o&nbsp;da&nbsp;expressÃ£o, o ator internacional pediu sinceras desculpas.</span><br />

<h2 class='date-header'><span>quinta-feira, 11 de abril de 2013</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry'>
<a name='3557090192798702898'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='http://www.celebrinando.com/2013/04/amds-chief-graphics-architect-really.html'>AMD&#8217;s chief graphics architect really likes the PlayStation 4</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-3557090192798702898'>
<br />
<div class="headline" style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; word-wrap: break-word;">
<h2 style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; clear: none; color: black; float: none; font-family: DinWeb; font-size: 26px; line-height: 1.1; margin: 0px 14px 10px 0px; padding: 0px; word-wrap: break-word;">
<img alt="The PlayStation 4\'s controller looks very similar to the PS3\'s." class="noscript-image" scale="0" src="http://postmediacanadadotcom.files.wordpress.com/2013/03/ps4controller.jpg?w=660&amp;h=330&amp;crop=1" style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; display: block; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; height: auto; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; max-width: 100%; width: 658.7926025390625px; word-wrap: break-word;" /></h2>
</div>
<figure style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin: 0px; word-wrap: break-word;"><figcaption style="box-sizing: border-box; margin-top: 7px !important; word-wrap: break-word;"><div class="story-feature-image-info" style="box-sizing: border-box; word-wrap: break-word;">
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span class="story-feature-image-credit" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #666666; display: block; font-size: 12px; line-height: 20px; margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px; text-transform: uppercase; word-wrap: break-word;"><b style="color: #333333; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; text-transform: none;"><a href="http://o.canada.com/2013/04/10/amds-chief-graphics-architect-really-likes-the-playstation-4/" target="_blank">Canada.com</a></b></span><span class="story-feature-image-credit" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #666666; display: block; font-size: 12px; line-height: 20px; margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px; text-transform: uppercase; word-wrap: break-word;"></span></span></div>
<div style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; text-transform: none; word-wrap: break-word;">
<div style="text-align: left;">
<span class="story-feature-image-credit" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #666666; display: block; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; line-height: 20px; margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px; text-transform: uppercase; word-wrap: break-word;"><span style="line-height: 20.909090042114258px;"><br /></span></span></div>
<div style="text-align: left;">
While at GDC, I had the chance to sit down and speak with AMD&#8217;s chief graphics product architect, John Gustafson.&nbsp;While he remained silent when it came to Microsoft&#8217;s next generation Xbox, he had a lot to say about Sony&#8217;s recently announced PlayStation 4.<br />
<div style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; word-wrap: break-word;">
&#8220;The PlayStation 4 blew me away but I&#8217;m conscious about being too positive about it because of course we have other partners that are competing,&#8221; said Gustafson at GDC (Game Developers Conference) in San Francisco.</div>
<div style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; word-wrap: break-word;">
During their big PlayStation 4 reveal back in February, Sony revealed that rather than creating their own hardware like they did with the PlayStation 3, the PlayStation 4 will adopt AMD created chipsets.</div>
<div style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; word-wrap: break-word;">
AMD also provides the graphics horsepower behind the Wii U, a fact Gustafson was quick to point out when asked about his feelings on the PlayStation 4 and the fact that it&#8217;s the only true next-generation console that&#8217;s been revealed so far. &#8220;Of course there is the Wii U too, we have AMD parts in there,&#8221; said Gustafson.</div>
<div class="wp-caption aligncenter" id="attachment_221910" style="background-color: white; border: 0px solid rgb(187, 187, 187); box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin: 5px auto; max-width: 96%; padding: 10px 10px 5px; text-align: center; width: 690px; word-wrap: break-word;">
<a href="http://postmediacanadadotcom.files.wordpress.com/2013/03/playstation.jpg" style="border: 0px; box-sizing: border-box; color: #666666; display: block; word-wrap: break-word;" target="_blank"><img alt="PlayStation GDC booth" class="size-large wp-image-221910" height="453" originalh="453" originalw="680" scale="1.5" src-orig="http://postmediacanadadotcom.files.wordpress.com/2013/03/playstation.jpg?w=680&amp;h=453" src="http://postmediacanadadotcom.files.wordpress.com/2013/03/playstation.jpg?w=818&amp;h=546" style="border: 0px none; box-sizing: border-box; display: inline-block; height: auto; margin: 0px; max-width: 100%; padding: 0px; word-wrap: break-word;" title="AMDs chief graphics architect really likes the PlayStation 4" width="680" /></a><br />
<div class="wp-caption-text" style="box-sizing: border-box; font-size: 13px; font-weight: bold; line-height: 14px; padding: 3px 0px 5px; text-align: left; word-wrap: break-word;">
Sony&#8217;s PlayStation booth on the GDC 2013 show floor.</div>
</div>
<div style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; word-wrap: break-word;">
He also seems to be very impressed with the specifications Sony has revealed so far about the PlayStation 4.</div>
<div style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; word-wrap: break-word;">
&#8220;It looks like they did an extremely good job of the engineering&#8230; The CPU and the GPU are on the same chip, which solves a lot of the problems (you don&#8217;t have to toss things over to a graphics card and try to get them back and forth).&#8221;</div>
<div style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; word-wrap: break-word;">
Going into specifics, Gustafson explained how he expects next generation physics engines on the PlayStation to be more realistic than we&#8217;ve ever seen before. He also emphasized that the console&#8217;s 8 GBs of ram will give developers a significant amount of breathing room when it comes to game development.</div>
<div style="background-color: white; box-sizing: border-box; color: #333333; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 13.63636302947998px; line-height: 20.909090042114258px; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-top: 1em; word-wrap: break-word;">
Gustafson also expanded on the potential he thinks the PS4 has when it comes to purposes outside of gaming, especially if it were used as some sort of server. According to him, all it would take is a few modifications and you&#8217;d have an amazing computer platform for all kinds of purposes.</div>
</div>
</div>
<span class="story-feature-image-credit" style="box-sizing: border-box; color: #666666; display: block; font-size: 12px; line-height: 20px; margin: 0px 10px 0px 0px; text-transform: uppercase; word-wrap: break-word;">
</span></div>
</figcaption></figure><br />
<b><a href="http://www.twitter.com/gamesreflexoes" target="_blank"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">@gamesreflexoes&nbsp;</span></a></b><br />

</div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: left; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;"><tbody>

<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: xx-small; text-align: start;"><b>"Verdade seja dita, adeptos da pirataria que nÃ£o pagam 180 reais agora,&nbsp;tambÃ©m&nbsp;nÃ£o pagarÃ£o quando for 100, 90, 80, 40...fato!"</b></span></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<br />
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Com a atual&nbsp;geraÃ§Ã£o&nbsp;de consoles de videogames, ficou mais&nbsp;difÃ­cil&nbsp;piratear jogos.&nbsp;InÃºmeras&nbsp;funcionalidades destes aparelhos&nbsp;sÃ£o&nbsp;perdidas quando o console sofre&nbsp;modificaÃ§Ãµes ilegais. Com isso a industria nacional oficial cresceu, ou melhor, passou a existir, pois quem acompanha o mercado sabe que ela praticamente&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;tinha parte no Brasil.&nbsp;</span><br />
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b>Veja abaixo nota da <a href="http://br.reuters.com/article/internetNews/idBRSPE92K06L20130321" target="_blank">Reuters Brasil</a></b></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<i><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><xhsgy style="background-color: white;"><b><span style="font-size: large;">"</span></b><span style="color: #990000;">O faturamento do mercado de&nbsp;consoles<xhsgy>&nbsp; de&nbsp;videogames&nbsp;no Brasil cresceu 43% em 2012 na comparaÃ§Ã£o anual, movimentando cerca de R$ 1 bilhÃ£o, de acordo com dados da empresa de pesquisa GfK divulgados nesta quinta-feira (21 de Mar</xhsgy></span></xhsgy></span><span style="color: #990000;"><span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Ã§</span><span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">o de 2013).</span><span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&nbsp;</span></span></i><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><i><span style="color: #990000;"><br style="background-color: white;" /><xhsgy style="background-color: white;">O avanÃ§o aconteceu apesar do brasileiro pagar caro pelos aparelhos - cerca de R$ 917 por&nbsp;console, bem cima, por exemplo, do valor mÃ©dio na Alemanha, de R$ 530 reais, segundo a GfK.&nbsp;</xhsgy><br style="background-color: white;" /><br style="background-color: white;" /><xhsgy style="background-color: white;">JÃ¡ o segmento de&nbsp;jogos&nbsp;movimentou R$ 629 milhÃµes no ano passado, alta de 72% sobre 2011, atribuÃ­da pela GfK Ã  "migraÃ§Ã£o de muitos consumidores para o mercado formal".&nbsp;</xhsgy><br style="background-color: white;" /><br style="background-color: white;" /><span style="background-color: white;">O preÃ§o dos jogos foi de, em mÃ©dia, R$ 103 no PaÃ­s, em linha com a mÃ©dia mundial, segundo a GfK. "O preÃ§o mÃ©dio nÃ£o caiu, jÃ¡ que o consumidor migrou para essa nova geraÃ§Ã£o e investiu em jogos e&nbsp;</span></span><span style="background-color: white;"><span style="color: #990000;">acessÃ³rios, especialmente os que permitem ficar de pÃ© e movimentar o corpo</span><b><span style="font-size: large;">"&nbsp;</span></b></span></i></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Hoje temos praticamente todas as grandes empresas de games representadas por aqui. Temos jogos dublados, legendados,&nbsp;lanÃ§amentos&nbsp;simultÃ¢neos, grandes eventos, e finalmente representamos de verdade uma fatia da industria mundial de jogos&nbsp;eletrÃ´nicos. Isso gerou empregos e principalmente a proximidade que os gamers tanto sonhavam.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Antes de qualquer coisa, esse texto&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;tem objetivo moralista. Mas comprar um produto original, seja um jogo ou qualquer outro,&nbsp;Ã© resultado de uma conscientizaÃ§Ã£o.&nbsp;VocÃª&nbsp;passa a entender que trata de uma&nbsp;questÃ£o&nbsp;simples, que&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Ã© o ato de</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&nbsp;pagar pelo que consome e de&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;contribuir para a&nbsp;expansÃ£o&nbsp;do crime de pirataria. Sem se conscientizar de tudo que isso envolve, fica muito difÃ­cil&nbsp;tentar convencer&nbsp;alguÃ©m&nbsp;se tratar de algo errado, pelo simples fato de praticamente&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;existir&nbsp;puniÃ§Ã£o&nbsp;para tal. Os filhos&nbsp;jÃ¡&nbsp;crescem vendo os pais nem sequer se importando com o assunto, consumindo todo tipo de "destrava"&nbsp;disponÃ­vel.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">A verdade&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Ã© que&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Ã© muito&nbsp;fÃ¡cil&nbsp;usar um produto ilegal, quase que 100%&nbsp;confortÃ¡vel, em termos de&nbsp;vocÃª eventualmente vir a ser preso e condenado por isso. Logo, o "mÃ©todo&nbsp;do medo" nÃ£o&nbsp;funciona aqui, ainda que deveria. Esta ligado em fazer a sua parte, e sabemos que quando fazemos nossa parte, a&nbsp;sensaÃ§Ã£o&nbsp;de que nada vai mudar aparece, ainda que ela&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;reflita a verdade, pois sua atitude faz sim a&nbsp;diferenÃ§a.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Escolher entre pagar a mensalidade da tv a cabo ao&nbsp;invÃ©s&nbsp;de pegar um "gato"&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;pode depender apenas da possibilidade real da policia bater na sua porta ou&nbsp;nÃ£o. Muitos nessa&nbsp;Ã©poca&nbsp;da internet se utilizam de um argumento "comunista" de que "toda cultura deve ser liberada", mas se esquecem que isso que eles chamam de cultura, na verdade&nbsp;sÃ£o&nbsp;negÃ³cios, e que se um comunista quiser de fato ser verdadeiro, deveria parar de consumir os produtos do capitalismo, mas claro que ninguÃ©m&nbsp;esta disposto a isso. Na verdade um adepto da pirataria se beneficia&nbsp;atravÃ©s&nbsp;das pessoas que pagam pelos&nbsp;serviÃ§os&nbsp;usados, como o caso da tv a cabo.</span><br />
<b><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span></b>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Claro, que dada a "cultura trapaceira" que a humanidade de um modo geral compartilha, a maioria das pessoas precisam de motivos alem do simples "dever moral",</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&nbsp;para fazer a coisa certa. E como estamos falando de games, listamos 6 razoes abaixo que&nbsp;irÃ£o&nbsp;fazer vocÃª&nbsp;no minimo entender, como isso faz total sentido.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>

<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Microsoft e Sony do Brasil, tem mostrado grande empenho em&nbsp;lanÃ§ar&nbsp;seus principais jogos em&nbsp;territÃ³rio&nbsp;nacional, legendando e dublando muitos deles em nosso idioma.&nbsp;Os principais lanÃ§amentos&nbsp;de <i>XBOX 360</i> e <i>PS3</i> tem custado em media 150 reais, valor bem aproximado dos justos 120 reais que falamos acima.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Existem&nbsp;tambÃ©m&nbsp;varias outras empresas e distribuidoras (NC Games, Warner, Nintendo, Synergex, Square Enix, Ubisoft e etc.), dispostas a desbravar este&nbsp;difÃ­cil&nbsp;territÃ³rio, e elas com certeza merecem nosso apoio. O recente <i>Assassin's Creed 3</i> por exemplo,&nbsp;jÃ¡&nbsp;esta oficialmente tabelado em apenas 99 reais. Caso contrario, os grandes eventos e&nbsp;lanÃ§amentos&nbsp;de games, irÃ£o permanecer como exclusividade internacional, e nos brasileiros, cada vez mais estaremos comendo apenas as migalhas que caem da mesa deles. Mas se&nbsp;vocÃª&nbsp;quer ver eventos como o&nbsp;jÃ¡&nbsp;popular e grande Brasil Game Show crescendo cada vez mais, esta ai o caminho.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Como vocÃª pode ver, existem 6 boas razÃµes para nÃ£o contribuir com a pirataria e optar pelo jogo original. Depende apenas da conscientizaÃ§Ã£o de quem realmente apoia e suporta a industria de games como um todo. Veja abaixo texto da ABES:</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<br />
<div style="border: 0px; color: #4f4f4f; margin-left: 32px; padding: 0px 0px 18px; width: 525px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">A pirataria de software age na contramÃ£o do crescimento econÃ´mico e da prosperidade do paÃ­s, contribuindo para o crime organizado e impedindo o crescimento de mercados, a geraÃ§Ã£o de empregos e a devida arrecadaÃ§Ã£o de tributos.</span></div>
<div style="border: 0px; color: #4f4f4f; margin-left: 32px; padding: 0px 0px 18px; width: 525px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">No Brasil, o atual Ã­ndice de pirataria de software Ã© considerado alarmante. A cada&nbsp;<strong style="border: 0px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">10</strong>&nbsp;programas adquiridos ou baixados pela internet em territÃ³rio nacional,&nbsp;<strong style="border: 0px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">mais de 5</strong>&nbsp;sÃ£o obtidos ilegalmente. Segundo estudo da BSA, a estimativa Ã© que, se e a taxa de pirataria diminuir 10 pontos percentuais (de 53% atualmente para 43%), R$ 6,4 bilhÃµes seriam adicionados Ã  economia local, 13 mil novos empregos seriam criados e aumentaria a receita da indÃºstria local em mais de R$ 4,8 bilhÃµes.</span></div>
<div style="border: 0px; color: #4f4f4f; margin-left: 32px; padding: 0px 0px 18px; width: 525px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Pirataria de software Ã© um assunto tÃ£o preocupante quanto exploraÃ§Ã£o do trabalho infantil, mÃ£o-de-obra escrava, falta de condiÃ§Ãµes sanitÃ¡rias adequadas ou agressÃ£o ao meio ambiente. Qualquer empresa que desrespeita fatores como estes pratica uma forma de concorrÃªncia desleal e traz prejuÃ­zos relevantes para todos em nosso paÃ­s.</span></div>
<div class="red" style="border: 0px; color: #cf0412; font-weight: bold; margin-left: 32px; padding: 0px 0px 18px; width: 525px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><a href="http://www.denunciepirataria.org.br/denounced" style="border: 0px; color: #cf0412; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none;" target="_blank">Seja um agente da mudanÃ§a. Denuncie casos de irregularidade!</a>&nbsp;</span></div>
<div class="red" style="border: 0px; color: #cf0412; font-weight: bold; margin-left: 32px; padding: 0px 0px 18px; width: 525px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><a href="http://www.denunciepirataria.org.br/home" target="_blank">Clique aqui.</a></span></div>
<div style="border: 0px; color: #4f4f4f; margin-left: 32px; padding: 0px 0px 18px; width: 525px;">
<strong style="border: 0px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Todos juntos por um Brasil mais Competitivo.</span></strong></div>
<br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Muitos que usam games piratas&nbsp;tambÃ©m&nbsp;usam o argumento de dizer que baixar musica na internet daria no mesmo que baixar jogos, bem,&nbsp;sÃ£o&nbsp;coisas bem diferentes.<span style="background-color: white;">&nbsp;O paragrafo abaixo&nbsp;</span>Ã© pra quem realmente se interessa pela&nbsp;questÃ£o.</span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: white;"><br /></span></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="background-color: white;">A</span></span><span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">tualmente todos cantores disponibilizam seus singles no <i>Youtube</i> pra quem quiser ouvir a hora que quiser, ate <i>Esse Cara Sou Eu</i> do Roberto Carlos, a Sony BMG&nbsp;disponibilizou&nbsp;la oficialmente. Os celulares hoje acessam internet, portanto baixar ou&nbsp;nÃ£o&nbsp;e&nbsp;sÃ³&nbsp;uma&nbsp;questÃ£o&nbsp;tÃ©cnica. Ja sobre series e filmes entra duas&nbsp;questÃµes&nbsp;para se encaixar na mesma&nbsp;questÃ£o&nbsp;citada sobre as musicas, uma&nbsp;</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Ã© se o programa&nbsp;</span><span style="background-color: white;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">passa nos canais da tv aberta ou fechada que&nbsp;vocÃª&nbsp;assina, portanto a pessoa&nbsp;jÃ¡&nbsp;paga por eles e ver na internet ou&nbsp;nÃ£o, nÃ£o&nbsp;faz&nbsp;diferenÃ§a&nbsp;alguma. O mesmo se aplica a programas que so sao transmitidos em outros paises.&nbsp;</span></span><br />
<span style="background-color: white;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br /></span></span>
<span style="background-color: white;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Lembrando que o objetivo do nosso texto nao&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Ã© convencer ninguem a nada, mas apenas trazer um ponto de vista. Obrigado por ler, e se gostou, divulgue em sua rede social escolhendo no icone logo abaixo.</span><br />

<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='http://www.celebrinando.com/2013/04/ps4-isnt-just-high-end-pc-says.html'>PS4 isn&#8217;t just a high-end PC, says Guerrilla Games</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-919344887626660835'>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13.333333015441895px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<a href="http://media.edge-online.com/wp-content/uploads/edgeonline/2013/04/Killzone4.jpg" rel="lightbox[82872]" style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; color: #ff10a3; font-family: inherit; font-size: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: none; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline;"><img alt="" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-82873" height="359" src="http://media.edge-online.com/wp-content/uploads/edgeonline/2013/04/Killzone4-610x343.jpg" style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px; font-family: inherit; font-size: inherit; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;" title="Killzone4" width="640" /></a></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<a href="http://www.edge-online.com/news/ps4-isnt-just-a-high-end-pc-says-guerrilla-games/" target="_blank"><b><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">By EDGE</span></b></a></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.7em;">Guerrilla Games&#8217; technical director Michiel Van Der Leeuw has dismissed the notion that PS4 is little more than a high-end PC, suggesting that those describing the console that way are &#8216;trolls&#8217; and &#8216;fanboys&#8217;.</span></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Speaking in an interview to be published in E253, on sale Thursday, Van Der Leeuw explained that his studio was heavily involved in the creation of PS4&#8217;s arcitecture, and while it might be more PC-like than its predecessor, it is still very much a games console.</span></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Referring to those calling PS4 a PC in a fancier box, he said: <b>&#8220;That&#8217;s difficult because people are trolling, right. What do you say to a troll? You don&#8217;t feed the trolls, that&#8217;ll make them grow.&#8221;</b></span></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<b><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">&#8220;I mean, it has always been a piece of high-end hardware that we put in a box, we find exactly the right components that complement each other and make a really good gaming experience. This is exactly the same thing &#8211; it is a console. The fact that the best pieces of hardware are also devised from, or optimised versions of, the stuff we find in PCs doesn&#8217;t make it any less a console. I can imagine if you find people with a vested interest to say PC gaming has won, they will find lots of great arguments in the fact that we use some of the same parts. But you know that&#8217;s just fanboys on the internet, I guess.&#8221;</span></b></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">Van Der Leeuw went on to explain the differences between PS4 and a high-powered PC. <b>&#8220;A PC is a number of parts which also has bridges in between where there are inefficiencies that may not be exactly the right match. We&#8217;ve got the right amount of memory, video card, everything balanced out. I know it was a very conscious effort to make sure that, with the speed of the memory, the amount of compute units, the speed of the hard-drive that we put in, that there would not be any bottlenecks. So the amount of pixel-pushers that you have, the amount of memory, the speed of your compute units make sure that you don&#8217;t hit any of the weakspots of the hardware.&#8221;</b></span></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">This balancing of PS4&#8217;s architecture and the use of complementary components make it simpler to work with, said Van Der Leeuw. <b>&#8220;Whereas if you have a PC very often your buffs, or your express buffs are very slow compared to your video RAM which is GDDR5 and your main RAM then is even slower than that, but you compensate by sticking buffers in there&#8230; there&#8217;s a lot of things to contemplate in the fact that it is a replaceable-parts architecture. This [PS4] is where all of the parts are designed to work together, naturally.&#8221;</b></span></div>
<div style="background-color: white; border: 0px; line-height: 1.7em; margin-bottom: 20px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">He added that Guerrilla was part of a constant iteration process with PS4&#8242;s innards. Guerrilla made&nbsp;at least five different major changes to the graphics chip, CPU and on the bandwidth between the different components, to define and then eliminate any disruption in performance.</span></div>
<span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.7em;"><b>&#8220;I think it was for more than a year that we knew the main ingredients and there was just discussion after discussion trying to find a bottleneck,&#8221; he added. &#8220;We actually had parts of both Killzone 3 and very early Killzone 4 art assets running through simulators to try to find out how it would behave on our speculative hardware that didn&#8217;t exist &#8211; trying to find bottlenecks in the hardware that we could fix before we could even think about the chip.&#8221;</b></span><br />
<span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.7em;"><b><br /></b></span>
<div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
<a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--ss8HxwOzIo/UWbTiCwmqWI/AAAAAAAADh8/tJmGhiZFvwE/s1600/cammy.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="484" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/--ss8HxwOzIo/UWbTiCwmqWI/AAAAAAAADh8/tJmGhiZFvwE/s640/cammy.jpg" width="640" /></a></div>
<span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.7em;"><b><br /></b></span>
<span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 1.7em;"><b><br /></b></span>
<br />
<h3 class="post-title entry-title" style="color: #111111; font-family: Arial, Tahoma, Helvetica, FreeSans, sans-serif; font-size: 19px; margin: 0px; position: relative;">

<h2 class='date-header'><span>sexta-feira, 5 de abril de 2013</span></h2>

          <div class="date-posts">
        
<div class='post-outer'>
<div class='post hentry'>
<a name='8803774861149980447'></a>
<h3 class='post-title entry-title'>
<a href='http://www.celebrinando.com/2013/04/why-ea-is-not-worst-company-in-america.html'>Why EA is not the &#8216;Worst Company in America&#8217; and Peter Moore is right</a>
</h3>
<div class='post-header'>
<div class='post-header-line-1'></div>
</div>
<div class='post-body entry-content' id='post-body-8803774861149980447'>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="float: left; margin-right: 1em; text-align: left;"><tbody>
<tr><td style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-WPZMNNcBY7Y/UV_0_vgRVQI/AAAAAAAADhg/CYrHfyp_hyg/s1600/ea-head-office-pic.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto;"><img border="0" height="476" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-WPZMNNcBY7Y/UV_0_vgRVQI/AAAAAAAADhg/CYrHfyp_hyg/s640/ea-head-office-pic.jpg" width="640" /></a></td></tr>
<tr><td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;"><span style="background-color: white; color: #444444; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: xx-small; line-height: 22px; text-align: start;"><b>"EA is not the main villain of this movie"</b></span></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<div style="background-color: white; margin-bottom: 24px; margin-right: 6px;">
<div style="line-height: 24px;">
<br /></div>
<div style="line-height: 24px;">
<span style="color: #444444; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 22px;"><br /></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">Jesus, this is so much hate! This is the internet after all, where people hide on their avatars to say bad things to others. This is not only about EA, but about Square Enix, Capcom, Activision, Apple, ABC, Fox, Justin Bieber, McDonalds, Twilight movies, Lady Gaga, Resident Evil, Call of Duty...EVERYTHING THAT IS POPULAR AND BIG, sadly human beings are jealous and hate the winners.&nbsp;</span></span><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;"><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">"Popular" = "People like it" (THIS IS WHAT MATTER in the entertainment world) , because "good" or "bad" is all about personal opinion and taste.</span></span><br />
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;"><br /></span></span>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">The winners have millions of fans, sure, loyal fans, but haters are always there too, side by side, to not respect the others taste (they say that is "no taste").&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">"The tallest trees catch the most wind" said Moore in the post.</span></span></div>
<div style="line-height: 24px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><br />
Electronic Arts COO&nbsp;<b>Peter Moore</b>&nbsp;has responded to a&nbsp;<a href="http://consumerist.com/2013/04/05/worst-company-in-america-semifinals-ea-vs-ticketmaster/" rel="nofollow" style="border: 0px none; color: #003399; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; resize: none; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline;" target="_blank">recent poll</a>&nbsp;in which EA was chosen as a semifinalist for &#8220;Worst Company in America.&#8221; (&nbsp;<a href="http://www.ign.com/articles/2012/06/14/why-do-people-hate-ea" style="border: 0px none; color: #003399; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; resize: none; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline;" target="_blank">also received last year</a>.) In a&nbsp;<a href="http://www.ea.com/news/we-can-do-better" rel="nofollow" style="background-color: transparent; border: 0px none; color: #003399; font-style: inherit; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; resize: none; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline;" target="_blank">blog post</a>&nbsp;called &#8220;We Can Do Better,&#8221; Moore explained that EA has made mistakes but went on to defend the company.&nbsp;</span></div>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 24px;"><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">Say what you want haters but EA still one of the best selling companies of the world, and we know that people love their games because they buy it every year. People don't buy what they really hate. Yes, EA make mistakes, but anyone is perfect. People can complain, sure, but with RESPECT. Remember: YOU STILL BUYING THEIR GAMES, EA is a huge company, so far beyond microtransaction. If EA is "milking" is because you are drinking and liking. If you don't like their products, don't buy it and shut up.&nbsp;</span></span><span style="color: #444444; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="line-height: 22px;">Haters are people that not understand that the world doesn't revolves around their personal taste. "I don't like it, then, this is a shit!".</span></span></div>
<div style="background-color: white; margin-bottom: 24px; margin-right: 6px;">
<div style="line-height: 24px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">If they have "absorbed" half of the good gaming companies from the industry, like some haters say, is because these companies were sold to them and both are making money,&nbsp;</span></span><span style="color: #444444; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', arial, sans-serif; line-height: 22px;">this is a good business for everyone, they need publisher EA to sell their games well, and without them and their ability to distribution, their games would be a flop. EA is not the main "villain" of this movie.</span><span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">&nbsp;It is "COD effect" all over again: Only hate on the internet and 25 millions copies sold every year.&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">Haters and public are different audiences, the public for example, play the demo and buy Resident Evil 6, but the haters go to Metacritic to give 1/10 to the game. They are not the same people.&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #444444; line-height: 22px;">Like Peter said on his post: "Every day, millions of people across globe play and love our games &#8211; literally, hundreds of millions more than will vote in this contest."</span></span></div>
<div>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 24px;"><span style="color: #444444;"><br /></span>
<span style="color: #444444;">Do you really think that this current business model, with many day one DLC and whatever, is a EA thing? This is the capitalism baby, and games, if you are 13 years old and don't know yet, IS BUSINESS too. And EA is right in many points because they, Ubisoft and Activision are the richer companies in the gaming industry today. And you are not obligated to buy anything from them, you are free to make your choice.&nbsp;</span></span><span style="color: #444444; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="line-height: 24px;">If they have money to buy a license, is because they deserve and have power to do this, and FIFA sold to them. Why don't you go complain with FIFA and NFL?</span></span><br />
<div style="line-height: 24px;">
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><span style="color: #444444;"><br /></span></span>
<span style="color: #444444; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', arial, sans-serif; line-height: 22px;">The first thing that you must understand is that no everyone hates the things that you hate. Which brings me to the next point: your arguments are valid, but they're only your point of view (which of course, is shared by many others). There are many people that think those games/singers/movies/companies are awesome. You cannot say that Twilight represents everything that is wrong with movies, because your point of view is not an universal truth. Another example: you and many may hate what Resident Evil has become, but clearly, many others enjoy it for a bunch of reasons.</span></div>
<div style="line-height: 24px;">
<span style="color: #444444; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 22px;"><br /></span><span style="color: #444444; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 22px;">If EA still selling millions of games every year there is a reason for that: SUCCESS. Like I say, and Peter Moore said about this too in his post, the huge sales, THIS is the real pool about a company. DEAL WITH IT!&nbsp;</span></div>
</div>
</div>
<span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;"><b>Mateus Prado Sousa</b> - <b><a href="http://www.twitter.com/gamesreflexoes" target="_blank">@gamesreflexoes&nbsp;</a></b></span>
<div style='clear: both;'></div>
</div>
